	<body>
		<category name="Atlas Reborn">
			<category name="Description">
				<comment>By Aaron0000</comment>
				<comment>Atlas Reborn</comment>
				<comment>Completely overhauls the Vladof manufacturer into Atlas from Borderlands 1.</comment>
				<category name="List of changes">
					<comment>All Vladof items (excluding class mods and some unique/seraph items) have been reskinned and renamed. This includes gemstone skins (now Orichalcum) and prefixes. Names are based off of Greek weapons and prefixes are based off of "superiority" as well as a few BL1 prefixes (List of Prefixes and Titles can be found below).</comment>
					<comment>Atlas Weapons have been globally rebalanced. The stats should be above average in all aspects.</comment>
					<comment>Most special weapons have been replaced or adjusted. Details down below.</comment>
					<comment>Atlas weapons have the feature of increasing action skill cooldown while held.</comment>
				</category>
				<category name="Notes">
					<comment>Already encorporates the GemstoneFixes mod for Vladof weapons.</comment>
					<comment>If using the community patch, load this file after the community patch. In general, load this file last.</comment>
					<comment>Chimera uses the splashes/explosions of the Twister and Hornet to achieve the desired effect. If a mod alters those splashes, it will affect the Chimera.</comment>
					<category name="Reticle">
						<comment>If you're having issues with reticles disappearing, it is a known issue. Due to gearbox wizardry, depending on the grip of a weapon, and the barrel of said weapon, the scoped view will have missing parts when using the Atlas logo. Find this line in the file:</comment>
						<comment>GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Vladof FlashLabelName Atlas</comment>
						<comment>and disable it or use Borderlands Community Mod Manager (BLCMM).</comment>
					</category>
				</category>
				<category name="Replacers & Renamings">
					<category name="Replacers">
						<comment>Infinity -> Chimera</comment>
						<comment>Shredifier -> Griffin</comment>
						<comment>Lyuda -> Cyclops</comment>
						<comment>Mongol -> Hydra</comment>
						<comment>Stinger -> Troll</comment>
						<comment>Patriot -> Argus</comment>
						<comment>Lead Storm -> Ogre</comment>
						<comment>Stalker -> Aries</comment>
						<comment>Rapier -> Ajax's Spear</comment>
						<comment>Veritas -> Erinyes</comment>
						<comment>Aequitas -> Shield of Heracles</comment>
						<category name="Details">
							<category name="Chimera">
								<comment>Always spawns in Fire versions (Does not remove other versions, but using non-Fire versions is not advised).</comment>
								<comment>Has Shock and Corrosive splash damage.</comment>
								<comment>Consumes two ammo per shot.</comment>
							</category>
							<category name="Griffon">
								<comment>Boosted base stats (Damage, accuracy, fire rate, magazine size, reload speed, recoil).</comment>
								<comment>Further boosted Action Skill cooldown.</comment>
								<comment>Increased projectile speed.</comment>
								<comment>Only spawns in elemental versions.</comment>
							</category>
							<category name="Cyclops">
								<comment>Always spawns with a Hyperion scope.</comment>
								<comment>Increased Critical Hit Damage.</comment>
								<comment>x11.2 Zoom.</comment>
								<comment>+30% damage.</comment>
								<comment>Reduced minimum spread.</comment>
								<comment>Increased accuracy when scoped.</comment>
								<comment>Doubled projectile speed.</comment>
								<comment>Produces transfusion orbs upon hitting an enemy.</comment>
							</category>
							<category name="Hydra">
								<comment>Fires five rockets in a horizontal spread.</comment>
								<comment>Actually does consume reduced ammo.</comment>
								<comment>Decreased damage per projectile.</comment>
								<comment>Increased accuracy.</comment>
							</category>
							<category name="Troll">
								<comment>Minor stat boosts.</comment>
								<comment>Increases damage resistance to all types while wielded (except fire).</comment>
								<comment>Grants health regeneration while held.</comment>
							</category>
							<category name="Argus">
								<comment>Behaves like a shotgun when hip-fired, and like a sniper rifle when aiming down sights.</comment>
								<comment>Decreased critical hit damage when hip-fired, increased critical damage when aiming down sights.</comment>
								<comment>Extended magazine capacity.</comment>
							</category>
							<category name="Ogre">
								<comment>Deals explosive damage regardless of element (Does not remove elemental versions, but always deals non-elemental damage on the bullet regardless. Using elemental versions will just lower the damage).</comment>
								<comment>Increased base damage.</comment>
								<comment>Significantly reduced spread.</comment>
								<comment>Heavily reduced recoil.</comment>
								<comment>Has a unique spread pattern.</comment>
							</category>
							<category name="Aries">
								<comment>Always spawns in shock (Does not remove non-shock versions that already exist, however.)</comment>
								<comment>Heavily boosted damage.</comment>
								<comment>Heavily reduced fire rate.</comment>
								<comment>Decreased spread.</comment>
								<comment>+100 Critical hit damage.</comment>
								<comment>Shooting an enemy will produce transfusion trails.</comment>
							</category>
							<category name="Ajax's Spear">
								<comment>Still has the same Melee effects as the Rapier. Just made it more effective as an actual gun.</comment>
								<comment>Increased base damage.</comment>
								<comment>Significantly reduced spread.</comment>
								<comment>Heavily reduced recoil.</comment>
							</category>
							<category name="Erinyes">
								<comment>60% increased fire rate.</comment>
								<comment>Burst-fires the entire magazine when the trigger is pulled.</comment>
								<comment>No bullet spread.</comment>
								<comment>Reduced damage.</comment>
								<comment>Longer reload times.</comment>
								<comment>No longer has the Aequitas-partner effect.</comment>
							</category>
							<category name="Shield of Heracles">
								<comment>Absorption shield with 50% elemental adapation resistance.</comment>
								<comment>No longer has the Veritas-partner effect.</comment>
							</category>
						</category>
					</category>
					<category name="Renamings">
						<comment>Sham -> Aegis</comment>
						<comment>Transformer -> Omega</comment>
						<comment>Sponge -> Leo</comment>
						<comment>Fire Bee -> Phoenix</comment>
						<comment>Storm Front -> Steropes</comment>
						<comment>Pandemic -> Python</comment>
					</category>
					<category name="Adjustments">
						<category name="Kitten">
							<comment>Gave Kitten a new, tighter spread and reduced the damage slightly to compensate.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Hail">
							<comment>Cut the arc of Hail in half.</comment>
						</category>
					</category>
				</category>
